A \" +\n146:         \"higher ratio will mean fewer, more efficient cleanings but will mean more wasted \" +\n147:         \"space in the log. If the \" + MAX_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG + \" or the \" + MIN_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG +\n148:         \" configurations are also specified, then the log compactor considers the log to be eligible for compaction \" +\n149:         \"as soon as either: (i) the dirty ratio threshold has been met and the log has had dirty (uncompacted) \" +\n150:         \"records for at least the \" + MIN_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG + \" duration, or (ii) if the log has had \" +\n151:         \"dirty (uncompacted) records for at most the \" + MAX_COMPACTION_LAG_MS_CONFIG + \" period.\";\n152: \n153:     public static final String CLEANUP_POLICY_CONFIG = \"cleanup.policy\";\n154:     public static final String CLEANUP_POLICY_COMPACT = \"compact\";\n155:     public static final String CLEANUP_POLICY_DELETE = \"delete\";\n156:     public static final String CLEANUP_POLICY_DOC = \"This config designates the retention policy to \" +\n157:         \"use on log segments. The \\\"delete\\\" policy (which is the default) will discard old segments \" +\n158:         \"when their retention time or size limit has been reached. The \\\"compact\\\" policy will enable \" +\n159:         \"<a href=\\\"#compaction\\\">log compaction</a>, which retains the latest value for each key. \" +\n160:         \"It is also possible to specify both policies in a comma-separated list (e.g. \\\"delete,compact\\\"). \" +\n161:         \"In this case, old segments will be discarded per the retention time and size configuration, \" +\n162:         \"while retained segments will be compacted.\";\n163: \n164:     public static final String UNCLEAN_LEADER_ELECTION_ENABLE_CONFIG = \"unclean.leader.election.enable\";\n165:     public static final String UNCLEAN_LEADER_ELECTION_ENABLE_DOC = \"Indicates whether to enable replicas \" +\n166:         \"not in the ISR set to be elected as leader as a last resort, even though doing so may result in data \" +\n167:         \"loss.<p>Note: In KRaft mode, when enabling this config dynamically, it needs to wait for the unclean leader election\" +\n168:         \"thread to trigger election periodically (default is 5 minutes). In the <code>acks=all</code> \" +\n174:         \"case, every in-sync replica must acknowledge a write for it to be considered successful. E.g., if a topic has \" +\n175:         \"<code>replication.factor</code> of 3 and the ISR set includes all three replicas, then all three replicas must acknowledge an \" +\n176:         \"<code>acks=all</code> write for it to succeed, even if <code>min.insync.replicas</code> happens to be less than 3. \" +\n177:         \"If <code>acks=all</code> and the current ISR set contains fewer than <code>min.insync.replicas</code> members, then the producer \" +\n178:         \"will raise an exception (either <code>NotEnoughReplicas</code> or <code>NotEnoughReplicasAfterAppend</code>).<br> \" +\n179:         \"Regardless of the <code>acks</code> setting, the messages will not be visible to the consumers until \" +\n180:         \"they are replicated to all in-sync replicas and the <code>min.insync.replicas</code> condition is met.<br> \" +\n181:         \"When used together, <code>min.insync.replicas</code> and <code>acks</code> allow you to enforce greater durability guarantees. \" +\n182:         \"A typical scenario would be to create a topic with a replication factor of 3, \" +\n183:         \"set <code>min.insync.replicas</code> to 2, and produce with <code>acks</code> of \\\"all\\\". \" +\n184:         \"This ensures that a majority of replicas must persist a write before it's considered successful by the producer and it's visible to consumers.\" +\n185:         \"<p>Note that when the Eligible Leader Replicas feature is enabled, the semantics of this config changes.
